Duration Legend
---------------
W - whole
H - half
Q - quarter
E - 8th
S - 16th
. - note dotted


Tablature Legend
----------------
NH - natural harmonic
^ - brush up
v - brush down

E - 8th
S - 16th
T - 32nd
X - 64th
. - note dotted
|-n-|  - n-tuplets


Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
b - bend
/ -  slide into from below or out of upwards
\ -  slide into from above or out of downwards
< - fade in
^ - brush up
v - brush down

Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
b - bend
~ - vibrato
W - wide vibrato
tr - trill
TP - tremolo picking
< - fade in
^ - brush up
v - brush down

Duration Legend
---------------
W - whole
H - half
Q - quarter
E - 8th
S - 16th
T - 32nd
X - 64th
. - note dotted
|-n-|  - n-tuplets


Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
b - bend
br - bendRelease
pb - preBend
pbr - preBendRelease
brb - bendReleaseBend
\n/ - tremolo bar dip
\n - tremolo bar dive
-/n - tremolo bar Release up
/n\ - tremolo bar inverted dip
/n - tremolo bar return
-\n - tremolo bar Release down
S - shift slide
s - legato slide
/ -  slide into from below or out of upwards
\ -  slide into from above or out of downwards
~ - vibrato
W - wide vibrato
tr - trill
TP - tremolo picking
T - tapping
S - slap
P - pop
< - fade in
^ - brush up
v - brush down

Title: Home
Artist: Toby Fox
Album: Undertale OST
Author: FeralCadence

Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
b - bend
/ -  slide into from below or out of upwards
\ -  slide into from above or out of downwards
< - fade in
^ - brush up
v - brush down

Duration Legend
---------------
W - whole
H - half
Q - quarter
E - 8th
S - 16th
T - 32nd
X - 64th
. - note dotted
|-n-|  - n-tuplets


Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
b - bend
br - bendRelease
pb - preBend
pbr - preBendRelease
brb - bendReleaseBend
\n/ - tremolo bar dip
\n - tremolo bar dive
-/n - tremolo bar Release up
/n\ - tremolo bar inverted dip
/n - tremolo bar return
-\n - tremolo bar Release down
S - shift slide
s - legato slide
/ -  slide into from below or out of upwards
\ -  slide into from above or out of downwards
~ - vibrato
W - wide vibrato
tr - trill
TP - tremolo picking
T - tapping
S - slap
P - pop
< - fade in
^ - brush up
v - brush down

Duration Legend
---------------
W - whole
H - half
Q - quarter
E - 8th
S - 16th
T - 32nd
X - 64th
. - note dotted
|-n-|  - n-tuplets


Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
b - bend
br - bendRelease
pb - preBend
pbr - preBendRelease
brb - bendReleaseBend
\n/ - tremolo bar dip
\n - tremolo bar dive
-/n - tremolo bar Release up
/n\ - tremolo bar inverted dip
/n - tremolo bar return
-\n - tremolo bar Release down
S - shift slide
s - legato slide
/ -  slide into from below or out of upwards
\ -  slide into from above or out of downwards
~ - vibrato
W - wide vibrato
tr - trill
TP - tremolo picking
T - tapping
S - slap
P - pop
< - fade in
^ - brush up
v - brush down

Duration Legend
---------------
W - whole
H - half
Q - quarter
E - 8th
S - 16th
T - 32nd
X - 64th
. - note dotted
|-n-|  - n-tuplets


Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
b - bend
br - bendRelease
pb - preBend
pbr - preBendRelease
brb - bendReleaseBend
\n/ - tremolo bar dip
\n - tremolo bar dive
-/n - tremolo bar Release up
/n\ - tremolo bar inverted dip
/n - tremolo bar return
-\n - tremolo bar Release down
S - shift slide
s - legato slide
/ -  slide into from below or out of upwards
\ -  slide into from above or out of downwards
~ - vibrato
W - wide vibrato
tr - trill
TP - tremolo picking
T - tapping
S - slap
P - pop
< - fade in
^ - brush up
v - brush down

Game: Undertale
by Toby Fox

----------------

x - dead note

h - hammer on

S - shift slide
s - legato slide

\ -  slide into from above or out of downwards
~ - vibrato
W - wide vibrato
tr - trill
< - fade in
^ - brush up
v - brush down

Chaos King                                              
Chaos King
Toby Fox
JordanVS

*Tuning: Drop D
Tempo: 148 ~ 4/4

This one looks messy on paper but it's pretty cool once you get the hang of it, I swear, so allow me to explain a few points:

1. Measures similar 4 or 6 should actually follow the bass rhythm on measures 1 or 3 but since I can`t play it like that I wrote the bass differently. In this case, the notes are supposed to grow in intensity together with the 2323 thingy.
2. I recommend playing the 00(0)s from measures 11 to 25 with your thumb, just strike it, don`t pluck it. I wouldn't play it too loud or let the open D string sound very clear either, but that`s just me.
3. The slides on measures 20 and 22 are supposed to sound messy. I like to play the melodies from this first section with expression, so with slides and some slight vibrato where I didn't write any. 
4. The chords on measures 29 and 33 are to be played with your thumb and muting the strings, it's ok if the bass note is played together. No need to play as many times as it's written, just fill the time with something.
5. The next section is just very difficult, I don't have anything else to add.

Download Link: https://www.mediafire.com/file/u8q1r79se3exphh/Chaos_King_-_Deltarune.zi...

Duration Legend
---------------
W - whole
H - half
Q - quarter
E - 8th
S - 16th
T - 32nd
X - 64th
. - note dotted
|-n-|  - n-tuplets


Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
/ -  slide into from below or out of upwards
\ -  slide into from above or out of downwards
^ - brush up
v - brush down


Chapter 1 - Short Pieces Medley                               
Deltarune
Toby Fox
JordanVS

A collection of every short piece from Chapter 1, just for completeness sake.

Download link: https://www.mediafire.com/file/rn9ckclpsv5kuvi/Short_Pieces_Medley_-_Del...

Duration Legend
---------------
W - whole
H - half
Q - quarter
E - 8th
S - 16th
T - 32nd
X - 64th
. - note dotted
|-n-|  - n-tuplets


Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
b - bend
br - bendRelease
pb - preBend
pbr - preBendRelease
brb - bendReleaseBend
S - shift slide
s - legato slide
/ -  slide into from below or out of upwards
\ -  slide into from above or out of downwards
~ - vibrato
W - wide vibrato
tr - trill
TP - tremolo picking
T - tapping
S - slap
P - pop
< - fade in
^ - brush up
v - brush down

Field of Hopes and Dreams                                           
Deltarune
Toby Fox
JordanVS

Once again, I made two versions of this tab: one with the capo and one without. 
Originally, I started the arrangement without the capo but that one proved to be a little too difficult (and annoying) to play, so I did an easier, less faithful version.
I also tried something different by adding more percussive elements in two different ways throughout the arrangements. 
Hopefully, it's clear how each of them should be played.

Tempo: 125 ~ 4/4

No capo:

Duration Legend
---------------
W - whole
H - half
Q - quarter
E - 8th
S - 16th
T - 32nd
X - 64th
. - note dotted
|-n-|  - n-tuplets


Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
^ - brush up
v - brush down

Album: 
Author: Arrangement: Eduardo Barelli

Duration Legend
---------------
W - whole
H - half
Q - quarter
E - 8th
S - 16th
T - 32nd
X - 64th
. - note dotted
|-n-|  - n-tuplets


Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
/ -  slide into from below or out of upwards
\ -  slide into from above or out of downwards
T - tapping
S - slap
P - pop
< - fade in
^ - brush up
v - brush down

Duration Legend
---------------
W - whole
H - half
Q - quarter
E - 8th
S - 16th
T - 32nd
X - 64th
. - note dotted
|-n-|  - n-tuplets


Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - echo-like repetition
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
^ - brush up
v - brush down

Tempo: 203 ~ 6/8 

The key was changed from Db to A. 
If you want to play it in the original key use a capo on the 4th fret. 
However, this arrangement wasn't created with a capo in mind so a few sections are a little awkward with it.

Duration Legend
---------------
W - whole
H - half
Q - quarter
E - 8th
S - 16th
T - 32nd
X - 64th
. - note dotted
|-n-|  - n-tuplets


Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
b - bend
br - bendRelease
pb - preBend
pbr - preBendRelease
brb - bendReleaseBend
\n/ - tremolo bar dip
\n - tremolo bar dive
-/n - tremolo bar Release up
/n\ - tremolo bar inverted dip
/n - tremolo bar return
-\n - tremolo bar Release down
S - shift slide
s - legato slide
/ -  slide into from below or out of upwards
\ -  slide into from above or out of downwards
~ - vibrato
W - wide vibrato
tr - trill
TP - tremolo picking
T - tapping
S - slap
P - pop
< - fade in
^ - brush up
v - brush down

Duration Legend
---------------
W - whole
H - half
Q - quarter
E - 8th
S - 16th
T - 32nd
X - 64th
. - note dotted
|-n-|  - n-tuplets


Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
S - shift slide
s - legato slide
~ - vibrato
W - wide vibrato
tr - trill
TP - tremolo picking
T - tapping
S - slap
P - pop
< - fade in
^ - brush up
v - brush down


My First Tab :3


Video of Tab (This tab is a credit to them. I just wanted to write it down): https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vHjacr-FhU8

BPM: 104

E = Eighth Note

Q = Quarter Note

H = Half Note

Duration Legend
---------------
W - whole
H - half
Q - quarter
E - 8th
S - 16th
. - note dotted
|-n-|  - n-tuplets


Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
/ -  slide into from below or out of upwards
\ -  slide into from above or out of downwards


THE WORLD REVOLVING
Deltarune
Toby Fox
JordanVS

I've taken some small liberties but I think it's pretty close to the original.
There's fingerings in the PDF for hard part on measures 19-20.
It's not too hard aside from that part but the truth is I'm starting to think the best way to play this song is by playing the melody with a very simple and calm accompaniment, like that one guy on youtube did. 
I didn't write it down like that because I believe it's easy enough to read the tab like this and figure out something on the spot. 

*Tuning: Half-Step Down (D# - G# - C# - F# - A# - d#)
Tempo: 95 ~ 2/4

Download Link:  https://www.mediafire.com/file/86modbsoscgeuqd/THE_WORLD_REVOLVING_-_Deltarune.zip/file

Duration Legend
---------------
W - whole
H - half
Q - quarter
E - 8th
S - 16th
T - 32nd
X - 64th
. - note dotted
|-n-|  - n-tuplets


Tablature Legend
----------------
L - tied note
x - dead note
g - grace note
(n) - ghost note
> - accentuded note
NH - natural harmonic
AH - artificial harmonic
TH - tapped harmonic
SH - semi harmonic
PH - pitch harmonic
h - hammer on
p - pull off
~ - vibrato
W - wide vibrato
tr - trill
T - tapping
S - slap
P - pop
< - fade in
^ - brush up
v - brush down
